+        function renderNonBuildingPanelContent(tabNum, item) {
+            const panel = document.getElementById(`detail-group-panel-${tabNum}`);
+            if (!panel) return;
+
+            const nbMeta = item.non_building_meta || {};
+            const formatKRW = (val) => {
+                if (!val || isNaN(val)) return "-";
+                if (val >= 100000000) {
+                    const eok = Math.floor(val / 100000000);
+                    const rest = Math.round((val % 100000000) / 10000);
+                    return rest > 0 ? `${eok}??${rest.toLocaleString()}留뚯썝` : `${eok}?듭썝`;
+                }
+                return `${Math.round(val / 10000).toLocaleString()}留뚯썝`;
+            };
+
+            if (tabNum === 2) {
+                let assetName = "?먯궛";

+import re
+
+def search_keywords(file_path, keywords):
+    encodings = ['utf-8', 'cp949', 'euc-kr', 'latin-1']
+    content = None
+    for enc in encodings:
+        try:
+            with open(file_path, 'r', encoding=enc) as f:
+                content = f.read()
+                print(f"Successfully loaded file with encoding: {enc}")
+                break
+        except Exception as e:
+            continue
+            
+    if content is None:
+        print("Failed to load file with any common encoding.")
+        return
+        
+    for kw in keywords:
+        matches = [m.start() for m in re.finditer(kw, content, re.IGNORECASE)]
+        print(f"\nKeyword '{kw}': Found {len(matches)} occurrences.")
+        for idx in matches[:15]:
+            start = max(0, idx - 100)
+            end = min(len(content), idx + 200)
+            snippet = content[start:end].replace('\n', ' [NL] ')
+            # Clean snippet for cp949 console printing
+            safe_snippet = ""
+            for char in snippet:
+                if ord(char) < 128:
+                    safe_snippet += char
+                else:
+                    safe_snippet += f"[{ord(char)}]"
+            print(f"  - Position {idx}: ... {safe_snippet} ...")
+
+search_keywords("mobile-app/src/screens/FeedScreen.tsx", ["ad", "banner", "adsense"])
+
+
+
+
+
+
+

+// ?곗떇 ?뚯떛 ?뚭퀬由ъ쬁 ?뚯뒪???ㅽ겕由쏀듃?낅땲??
+// index.html???묒꽦??extractNonBuildingMeta ?⑥닔瑜??숈씪?섍쾶 媛?몄? ?ㅼ뼇???좏삎??李⑤웾 ?쒕ぉ怨?蹂몃Ц?????寃?ы빀?덈떎.
+
+function extractNonBuildingMeta(text, ptype, title) {
+    const meta = {};
+    if (!text) return meta;
+    const p_clean = (ptype || "").toLowerCase();
+    const text_clean = text.replace(/\n/g, " ").replace(/\s\s+/g, " ").trim();
+    
+    const isVehicle = p_clean.includes("李⑤웾") || p_clean.includes("?먮룞李?) || p_clean.includes("以묎린") || p_clean.includes("?좊컯") || p_clean.includes("??났湲?) || p_clean.includes("?댁넚") || p_clean.includes("吏寃뚯감") || p_clean.includes("?λ퉬");
+    
+    let yearVal = null;
+    if (title) {
+        const title_clean = title.replace(/\n/g, " ").replace(/\s\s+/g, " ").trim();
+        
+        // 1. 4?먮━ ?곕룄 留ㅼ묶
+        const year4StrictMatch = title_clean.match(/(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\s*(?:?꾩떇|?꾪삎|???쒖옉)/i);
+        if (year4StrictMatch) {
+            yearVal = year4StrictMatch[1] + "?꾩떇";
+        }
+        
+        // 2. 2?먮━ ?곕룄 留ㅼ묶 諛??멸린 ?먮룞 蹂댁젙
+        if (!yearVal) {
+            const year2Match = title_clean.match(/(\d{2})\s*(?:?꾩떇|?꾪삎|??/i);
+            if (year2Match) {
+                let yearNum = parseInt(year2Match[1]);
+                if (yearNum >= 80 && yearNum <= 99) {
+                    yearVal = (1900 + yearNum) + "?꾩떇";
+                } else {
+                    yearVal = (2000 + yearNum) + "?꾩떇";
+                }
+            }
+        }
+        
+        // 3. 愿꾪샇 ?덉쓽 ?곕룄 媛먯?
+        if (!yearVal) {
+            const parenMatch = title_clean.match(/\((20\d{2}|19\d{2}|\d{2})\s*(?:?꾩떇|?꾪삎|???\)/i);
+            if (parenMatch) {
+                let val = parenMatch[1];
+                if (val.length === 2) {
+                    let yearNum = parseInt(val);
+                    if (yearNum >= 80 && yearNum <= 99) {
+                        yearVal = (1900 + yearNum) + "?꾩떇";
+                    } else {
+                        yearVal = (2000 + yearNum) + "?꾩떇";
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    yearVal = val + "?꾩떇";
+                }
+            }
+        }
+
+        // 4. ?쇰컲 4?먮━ ?곕룄 ?⑤룆 留ㅼ묶
+        if (!yearVal) {
+            const simpleYearMatch = title_clean.match(/\b(19\d{2}|20\d{2})\b/);
+            if (simpleYearMatch) {
+                const idx = simpleYearMatch.index;
+                const beforeStr = title_clean.substring(Math.max(0, idx - 10), idx);
+                const afterStr = title_clean.substring(idx + 4, Math.min(title_clean.length, idx + 15));
+                if (!beforeStr.includes("?寃?) && !afterStr.includes("?寃?) && !beforeStr.includes("愿由щ쾲??) && !afterStr.includes("-") && !beforeStr.includes("/")) {
+                    yearVal = simpleYearMatch[1] + "?꾩떇";
+                }
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    const keywordsMap = {
+        base_location: ['?ъ슜蹂멸굅吏', '?ъ슜 蹂멸굅吏', '蹂멸굅吏'],
+        vehicle_no: ['?깅줉踰덊샇', '李⑤웾?깅줉踰덊샇', '李⑤웾踰덊샇', '?깅줉 踰덊샇'],
+        model_name: ['李⑤챸', '紐⑤뜽紐?, '李?紐?, '紐⑤뜽 紐?],
+        model_year: ['?곗떇', '????, '?쒖옉?꾨룄', '?쒖옉?곕룄', '?쒖옉 ?꾨룄', '?쒖옉 ?곕룄', '????'],
+        vehicle_type: ['李⑥쥌', '李?醫?],
+        vin: ['李⑤?踰덊샇', '李⑤? 踰덊샇'],
+        engine_type: ['?먮룞湲고삎??, '?먮룞湲??뺤떇', '?먮룞湲?],
+        storage_location: ['蹂닿??μ냼', '蹂닿? ?μ냼', '蹂닿?吏', '?뚯옱吏', '蹂닿?'],
+        spec_no: ['?쒖썝愿由щ쾲??, '?쒖썝 愿由щ쾲??, '愿由щ쾲??, '?쒖썝踰덊샇'],
+        fuel: ['?곕즺', '??猷?],
+        displacement: ['諛곌린??, '諛곌린 ??],
+        color: ['?됱긽', '????]
+    };
+
+    const matches = [];
+    for (const [key, aliases] of Object.entries(keywordsMap)) {
+        for (const alias of aliases) {
+            const regexStr = alias.replace(/\s+/g, "\\s*") + "\\s*:\\s*";
+            const regex = new RegExp(regexStr, "gi");
+            let match;
+            while ((match = regex.exec(text_clean)) !== null) {
+                matches.push({ key: key, alias: alias, start: match.index, end: regex.lastIndex });
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    matches.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start);
+    const filteredMatches = [];
+    let lastEnd = -1;
+    for (const m of matches) {
+        if (m.start >= lastEnd) {
+            filteredMatches.push(m);
+            lastEnd = m.end;
+        }
+    }
+
+    const parsed = {};
+    for (let i = 0; i < filteredMatches.length; i++) {
+        const current = filteredMatches[i];
+        const next = filteredMatches[i + 1];
+        const valueStart = current.end;
+        const valueEnd = next ? next.start : text_clean.length;
+        let value = text_clean.substring(valueStart, valueEnd).trim();
+        value = value.replace(/^[,\s:|#;]+|[,\s:|#;]+$/g, "").trim();
+        parsed[current.key] = value;
+    }
+
+    if (isVehicle) {
+        meta.asset_type = "vehicle";
+        meta.model_year = yearVal || (parsed.model_year ? (parsed.model_year.includes("??) ? parsed.model_year : parsed.model_year + "?꾩떇") : null);
+        meta.vehicle_no = parsed.vehicle_no || null;
+        meta.model_name = parsed.model_name || null;
+    }
+    return meta;
+}
